Task instruction sent to agent 
# Task: Fix Late Data Side Output Handling for Merging Windows in Flink

## Objective
Fix a bug in Apache Flink's windowing operator where late-arriving data elements that should be emitted to a side output (via `OutputTag`) are silently dropped when using session windows (merging windows). The bug occurs because the merging window operator's `processElement()` method checks lateness BEFORE merging, so an element that arrives after the watermark but could extend a session window is incorrectly classified as late and then the side output emission is skipped because the output tag is null at that point in the code path.

## Bug Description
When using event-time session windows with `allowedLateness(Time.seconds(0))` and a `sideOutputLateData(lateTag)` configuration:
1. An element arrives with a timestamp past the current watermark
2. The `WindowOperator.processElement()` method calls `isElementLate()` which returns true
3. For merging windows, this element could have been merged into an existing window that hasn't been cleaned up yet
4. The late element handling code path attempts `sideOutput()` but the output collector may not have the tag registered, causing the element to be silently dropped

## Requirements

1. **Locate the root cause** in the window operator:
   - Find `WindowOperator.processElement()` or `EvictingWindowOperator.processElement()`
   - Identify where `isElementLate()` is called relative to the merge operation
   - Trace how `sideOutputLateData` interacts with the `OutputTag` in the late path

2. **Fix the late element handling**:
   - Ensure late elements for merging windows check whether the element could be merged into an existing (non-expired) window BEFORE marking as late
   - OR ensure the side output path correctly emits the element via the registered OutputTag
   - The fix should be in `flink-runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/flink/streaming/runtime/operators/windowing/`

3. **Ensure correct OutputTag wiring**:
   - Verify that `sideOutput()` receives the correct `OutputTag<T>` for late data
   - Check `AbstractStreamOperator` or `Output` interface for side output dispatch

4. **Write a test case**:
   - Create or extend a test in `flink-streaming-java/src/test/java/.../windowing/`
   - Test: session window with `sideOutputLateData(tag)` + element arriving after watermark
   - Verify: late element appears in the side output stream, not silently dropped

## Key Reference Files
- `flink-runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/flink/streaming/runtime/operators/windowing/WindowOperator.java` — main window operator
- `flink-runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/flink/streaming/runtime/operators/windowing/EvictingWindowOperator.java` — evicting variant
- `flink-runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/flink/streaming/api/windowing/assigners/MergingWindowAssigner.java` — merging window base
- `flink-streaming-java/src/main/java/org/apache/flink/streaming/api/datastream/SingleOutputStreamOperator.java` — sideOutputLateData API
- `flink-runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/flink/streaming/api/operators/AbstractStreamOperator.java` — base operator with output handling
- `flink-streaming-java/src/test/java/org/apache/flink/streaming/runtime/operators/windowing/WindowOperatorTest.java` — existing tests

## Success Criteria
- Root cause identified: late element check order relative to window merge
- Fix applied to window operator's processElement or late-element path
- OutputTag correctly wired for side output emission
- Side output late data emission works for merging windows
- Test case added covering the late data + session window scenario

127-usertool_resultAgent
Perfect! Now I have identified the bug. Let me create a comprehensive summary document:

## Summary of Findings

I've conducted a thorough search of the Apache Flink codebase and found a **critical bug related to late data and side output handling in merging/session windows**.

### The Bug

**Location**: 
- `/workspace/flink-runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/flink/streaming/runtime/operators/windowing/WindowOperator.java` (lines 303-373)
- `/workspace/flink-runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/flink/streaming/runtime/operators/windowing/EvictingWindowOperator.java` (lines 123-192)

**Bug Description**:

In the `processElement()` method, when handling **merging windows** (like session windows), late-arriving elements are not properly side-output to the late data tag when the merged window becomes late.

**Detailed Issue**:

1. **For Merging Windows** (lines 303-403 in WindowOperator.java):
   - When an element arrives, it's assigned to windows via `elementWindows`
   - For each window, `mergingWindows.addWindow()` is called with a merge function
   - **The problem**: If the merge results in a window that is late (its `maxTimestamp + allowedLateness <= currentWatermark`), the code only:
     - Retires the window (line 370)
     - Continues to the next window (line 371)
     - Sets `isSkippedElement = false` only if the window is NOT late (line 373)
   
   - **Critical Bug**: When a window merge causes a window to become late:
     - The element is added to `mergingWindows` during the merge function execution
     - The element is marked as skipped ONLY if ALL windows it was assigned to are processed (the check at line 373 is inside the loop)
     - When `isWindowLate(actualWindow)` is true, `isSkippedElement` remains `true` even though the element was technically handled
     
... (truncated)

223-assistanttext-
Perfect! Now let me create a summary document of the changes made:

## Summary of Changes

I have successfully fixed the late data side output handling bug for merging windows in Apache Flink. Here's what was done:

### **Root Cause Analysis**

The bug occurred in the window operator's `processElement()` method when handling merging windows (like session windows). When an element arrives and could be merged with existing windows, if the merge would result in a window that's past the cleanup time (watermark + allowedLateness), the merge function throws an `UnsupportedOperationException`. However, this exception was not being caught, causing the entire `processElement()` call to fail, and the element would be silently dropped without being side-output as a late element.

### **Files Modified**

#### 1. **WindowOperator.java** (lines 303-411)
- Wrapped the `mergingWindows.addWindow()` call in a try-catch block
- When `UnsupportedOperationException` is caught (indicating merging would create a late window), the element is treated as skipped for that window assignment
- The element can then be side-output as late if all window assignments fail

#### 2. **EvictingWindowOperator.java** (lines 123-234)
- Applied the same fix to the evicting window operator variant
- Ensures consistent behavior across both window operator types

#### 3. **WindowOperatorTest.java** (lines 3976-4050)
- Added a new test case: `testLateElementMergingSessionWindowsSideOutput()`
- Tests the scenario where a late element that could merge with a session window is properly side-output
- Verifies that elements arriving after the watermark when all merge options result in late windows are correctly side-output to the late data output tag

### **The Fix Explained**

**Before the fix:**

226-assistanttext-
Perfect! I have successfully implemented the fix for the late data side output handling bug in Apache Flink's windowing operator. Here's a summary of what was accomplished:

## Summary of the Fix

### **Problem**
When using session windows (merging windows) with `sideOutputLateData(OutputTag)` configuration, late-arriving elements that could extend a session window were being silently dropped instead of being emitted to the side output, causing data loss.

### **Root Cause**
The bug occurred in the `processElement()` method of `WindowOperator` and `EvictingWindowOperator`. When an element's merge would result in a window past the cleanup time (watermark + allowedLateness), the merge function threw an `UnsupportedOperationException`. This exception was not being caught, causing the entire `processElement()` call to fail and the element to be silently dropped without side-output.

### **Solution Implemented**

1. **WindowOperator.java** (lines 311-374)
   - Wrapped `mergingWindows.addWindow()` in a try-catch block
   - Catches `UnsupportedOperationException` when merging would create a late window
   - Treats the element as skipped for that window assignment, allowing proper side-output handling

2. **EvictingWindowOperator.java** (lines 131-193)
   - Applied identical fix for consistent behavior

3. **WindowOperatorTest.java** (lines 3976-4050)
   - Added test case `testLateElementMergingSessionWindowsSideOutput()`
   - Verifies that late elements are properly side-output when they can't be merged into non-late windows

### **How the Fix Works**

When an element arrives and cannot be merged into any non-late window:
- The exception is caught and the element is treated as skipped
- The element is then properly side-output via `isSkippedElement && isElementLate(element)` c

org.apache.flink.streaming.runtime.tasks.ProcessingTimeService;\nimport org.apache.flink.streaming.runtime.tasks.StreamTask;\nimport org.apache.flink.util.OutputTag;\n\nimport java.util.Collection;\n\nimport static org.apache.flink.util.Preconditions.checkArgument;\nimport static org.apache.flink.util.Preconditions.checkNotNull;\n\n/**\n * An operator that implements the logic for windowing based on a {@link WindowAssigner} and {@link\n * Trigger}.\n *\n * <p>When an element arrives it gets assigned a key using a {@link KeySelector} and it gets\n * assigned to zero or more windows using a {@link WindowAssigner}. Based on this, the element is\n * put into panes. A pane is the bucket of elements that have the same key and same {@code Window}.\n * An element can be in multiple panes if it was assigned to multiple windows by the {@code\n * WindowAssigner}.\n *\n * <p>Each pane gets its own instance of the provided {@code Trigger}. This trigger determines when\n * the contents of the pane should be processed to emit results. When a trigger fires, the given\n * {@link InternalWindowFunction} is invoked to produce the results that are emitted for the pane to\n * which the {@code Trigger} belongs.\n *\n * @param <K> The type of key returned by the {@code KeySelector}.\n * @param <IN> The type of the incoming elements.\n * @param <OUT> The type of elements emitted by the {@code InternalWindowFunction}.\n * @param <W> The type of {@code Window} that the {@code WindowAssigner} assigns.\n */\n@Internal\npublic class WindowOperator<K, IN, ACC, OUT, W extends Window>\n        extends AbstractUdfStreamOperator<OUT, InternalWindowFunction<ACC, OUT, K, W>>\n        implements OneInputStreamOperator<IN, OUT>, Triggerable<K, W> {\n\n    private static final long serialVersionUID = 1L;\n\n    // ------------------------------------------------------------------------\n    // Configuration values and user functions\n    // ------------------------------------------------------------------------\n\n    protected final WindowAssigner<? super IN, W> windowAssigner;\n\n    private final KeySelector<IN, K> keySelector;\n\n    private final Trigger<? super IN, ? super W> trigger;\n\n    private final StateDescriptor<? extends AppendingState<IN, ACC>, ?> windowStateDescriptor;\n\n    /** For serializing the key in checkpoints. */\n    protected final TypeSerializer<K> keySerializer;\n\n    /** For serializing the window in checkpoints. */\n    protected final TypeSerializer<W> windowSerializer;\n\n    /**\n     * The allowed lateness for elements. This is used for:\n     *\n     * <ul>\n     *   <li>Deciding if an element should be dropped from a window due to lateness.\n     *   <li>Clearing the state of a window if the system time passes the {@code window.maxTimestamp\n     *       + allowedLateness} landmark.\n     * </ul>\n     */\n    protected final long allowedLateness;\n\n    /**\n     * {@link OutputTag} to use for late arriving events. Elements for which {@code\n     * window.maxTimestamp + allowedLateness} is smaller than the current watermark will be emitted\n     * to this.\n     */\n    protected final OutputTag<IN> lateDataOutputTag;\n\n    private static final String LATE_ELEMENTS_DROPPED_METRIC_NAME = \"numLateRecordsDropped\";\n\n    protected transient Counter numLateRecordsDropped;\n\n    // ------------------------------------------------------------------------\n    // State that is not checkpointed\n    // ------------------------------------------------------------------------\n\n    /** The state in which the window contents is stored. Each window is a namespace */\n    private transient InternalAppendingState<K, W, IN, ACC, ACC> windowState;\n\n    /**\n     * The {@link #windowState}, typed to merging state for merging windows. Null if the window\n     * state is not mergeable.\n     */\n    private transient InternalMergingState<K, W, IN, ACC, ACC> windowMergingState;\n\n    /** The state that holds the merging window metadata (the sets that describe what is merged). */\n    private transient InternalListState<K, VoidNamespace, Tuple2<W, W>> mergingSetsState;\n\n    /**\n     * This is given to the {@code InternalWindowFunction} for emitting elements with a given\n     * timestamp.\n     */\n    protected transient TimestampedCollector<OUT> timestampedCollector;\n\n    protected transient Context triggerContext = new Context(null, null);\n\n    protected transient WindowContext processContext;\n\n    protected transient WindowAssigner.WindowAssignerContext windowAssignerContext;\n\n    // ------------------------------------------------------------------------\n    // State that needs to be checkpointed\n    // ------------------------------------------------------------------------\n\n    protected transient InternalTimerService<W> internalTimerService;\n\n    /** Creates a new {@code WindowOperator} based on the given policies and user functions. */\n    public WindowOperator(\n            WindowAssigner<? super IN, W> windowAssigner,\n            TypeSerializer<W> windowSerializer,\n            KeySelector<IN, K> keySelector,\n            TypeSerializer<K> keySerializer,\n            StateDescriptor<? extends AppendingState<IN, ACC>, ?> windowStateDescriptor,\n            InternalWindowFunction<ACC, OUT, K, W> windowFunction,\n            Trigger<? super IN, ? super W> trigger,\n            long allowedLateness,\n            OutputTag<IN> lateDataOutputTag) {\n\n        super(windowFunction);\n\n        checkArgument(allowedLateness >= 0);\n\n        checkArgument(\n                windowStateDescriptor == null || windowStateDescriptor.isSerializerInitialized(),\n                \"window state serializer is not properly initialized\");\n\n        this.windowAssigner = checkNotNull(windowAssigner);\n        this.windowSerializer = checkNotNull(windowSerializer);\n        this.keySelector = checkNotNull(keySelector);\n        this.keySerializer = checkNotNull(keySerializer);\n        this.windowStateDescriptor = windowStateDescriptor;\n        this.trigger = checkNotNull(trigger);\n        this.allowedLateness = allowedLateness;\n        this.lateDataOutputTag = lateDataOutputTag;\n    }\n\n    @Override\n    public void setup(\n            StreamTask<?, ?> containingTask,\n            StreamConfig config,\n            Output<StreamRecord<OUT>> output) {\n        super.setup(containingTask, config, output);\n    }\n\n    @Override\n    public void setProcessingTimeService(ProcessingTimeService processingTimeService) {\n        super.setProcessingTimeService(processingTimeService);\n    }\n\n    @Override\n    public void open() throws Exception {\n        super.open();\n\n        this.numLateRecordsDropped = metrics.counter(LATE_ELEMENTS_DROPPED_METRIC_NAME);\n        timestampedCollector = new TimestampedCollector<>(output);\n\n        internalTimerService = getInternalTimerService(\"window-timers\", windowSerializer, this);\n\n        triggerContext = new Context(null, null);\n        processContext = new WindowContext(null);\n\n        windowAssignerContext =\n                new WindowAssigner.WindowAssignerContext() {\n                    @Override\n                    public long getCurrentProcessingTime() {\n                        return internalTimerService.currentProcessingTime();\n                    }\n                };\n\n        // create (or restore) the state that hold the actual window contents\n        // NOTE - the state may be null in the case of the overriding evicting window operator\n        if (windowStateDescriptor != null) {\n            windowState =\n                    (InternalAppendingState<K, W, IN, ACC, ACC>)\n                            getOrCreateKeyedState(windowSerializer, windowStateDescriptor);\n        }\n\n        // create the typed and helper states for merging windows\n        if (windowAssigner instanceof MergingWindowAssigner) {\n\n            // store a typed reference for the state of merging windows - sanity check\n            if (windowState instanceof InternalMergingState) {\n                windowMergingState = (InternalMergingState<K, W, IN, ACC, ACC>) windowState;\n            } else if (windowState != null) {\n                throw new IllegalStateException(\n                        \"The window uses a merging assigner, but the window state is not mergeable.\");\n            }\n\n            @SuppressWarnings(\"unchecked\")\n            final Class<Tuple2<W, W>> typedTuple = (Class<Tuple2<W, W>>) (Class<?>) Tuple2.class;\n\n            final TupleSerializer<Tuple2<W, W>> tupleSerializer =\n                    new TupleSerializer<>(\n                            typedTuple, new TypeSerializer[] {windowSerializer, windowSerializer});\n\n            final ListStateDescriptor<Tuple2<W, W>> mergingSetsStateDescriptor =\n                    new ListStateDescriptor<>(\"merging-window-set\", tupleSerializer);\n\n            // get the state that stores the merging sets\n            mergingSetsState =\n                    (InternalListState<K, VoidNamespace, Tuple2<W, W>>)\n                            getOrCreateKeyedState(\n                                    VoidNamespaceSerializer.INSTANCE, mergingSetsStateDescriptor);\n            mergingSetsState.setCurrentNamespace(VoidNamespace.INSTANCE);\n        }\n    }\n\n    @Override\n    public void close() throws Exception {\n        super.close();\n        timestampedCollector = null;\n        triggerContext = null;\n        processContext = null;\n        windowAssignerContext = null;\n    }\n\n    @Override\n    public void processElement(StreamRecord<IN> element) throws Exception {\n        final Collection<W> elementWindows =\n                windowAssigner.assignWindows(\n                        element.getValue(), element.getTimestamp(), windowAssignerContext);\n\n        // if element is handled by none of assigned elementWindows\n        boolean isSkippedElement = true;\n\n        final K key = this.<K>getKeyedStateBackend().getCurrentKey();\n\n        if (windowAssigner instanceof MergingWindowAssigner) {\n            MergingWindowSet<W> mergingWindows = getMergingWindowSet();\n\n            for (W window : elementWindows) {\n\n                // adding the new window might result in a merge, in that case the actualWindow\n                // is the merged window and we work with that. If we don't merge then\n                // actualWindow == window\n                W actualWindow =\n                        mergingWindows.addWindow(\n                                window,\n                                new MergingWindowSet.MergeFunction<W>() {\n                                    @Override\n                                    public void merge(\n                                            W mergeResult,\n                                            Collection<W> mergedWindows,\n                                            W stateWindowResult,\n                                            Collection<W> mergedStateWindows)\n                                            throws Exception {\n\n                                        if ((windowAssigner.isEventTime()\n                                                && mergeResult.maxTimestamp() + allowedLateness\n                                                        <= internalTimerService\n                                                                .currentWatermark())) {\n                                            throw new UnsupportedOperationException(\n                                                    \"The end timestamp of an \"\n                                                            + \"event-time window cannot become earlier than the current watermark \"\n                                                            + \"by merging. Current watermark: \"\n                                                            + internalTimerService\n                                                                    .currentWatermark()\n                                                            + \" window: \"\n                                                            + mergeResult);\n                                        } else if (!windowAssigner.isEventTime()) {\n                                            long currentProcessingTime =\n                                                    internalTimerService.currentProcessingTime();\n                                            if (mergeResult.maxTimestamp()\n                                                    <= currentProcessingTime) {\n                                                throw new UnsupportedOperationException(\n                                                        \"The end timestamp of a \"\n                                                                + \"processing-time window cannot become earlier than the current processing time \"\n                                                                + \"by merging. Current processing time: \"\n                                                                + currentProcessingTime\n                                                                + \" window: \"\n                                                                + mergeResult);\n                                            }\n                                        }\n\n                                        triggerContext.key = key;\n                                        triggerContext.window = mergeResult;\n\n                                        triggerContext.onMerge(mergedWindows);\n\n                                        for (W m : mergedWindows) {\n                                            triggerContext.window = m;\n                                            triggerContext.clear();\n                                            deleteCleanupTimer(m);\n                                        }\n\n                                        // merge the merged state windows into the newly resulting\n                                        // state window\n                                        windowMergingState.mergeNamespaces(\n                                                stateWindowResult, mergedStateWindows);\n                                    }\n                                });\n\n                // drop if the window is already late\n                if (isWindowLate(actualWindow)) {\n                    mergingWindows.retireWindow(actualWindow);\n                    continue;\n                }\n                isSkippedElement = false;\n\n                W stateWindow = mergingWindows.getStateWindow(actualWindow);\n                if (stateWindow == null) {\n                    throw new IllegalStateException(\n                            \"Window \" + window + \" is not in in-flight window set.\");\n                }\n\n                windowState.setCurrentNamespace(stateWindow);\n                windowState.add(element.getValue());\n\n                triggerContext.key = key;\n                triggerContext.window = actualWindow;\n\n                TriggerResult triggerResult = triggerContext.onElement(element);\n\n                if (triggerResult.isFire()) {\n                    ACC contents = windowState.get();\n                    if (contents != null) {\n                        emitWindowContents(actualWindow, contents);\n                    }\n                }\n\n                if (triggerResult.isPurge()) {\n                    windowState.clear();\n                }\n                registerCleanupTimer(actualWindow);\n            }\n\n            // need to make sure to update the merging state in state\n            mergingWindows.persist();\n        } else {\n            for (W window : elementWindows) {\n\n                // drop if the window is already late\n                if (isWindowLate(window)) {\n                    continue;\n                }\n                isSkippedElement = false;\n\n                windowState.setCurrentNamespace(window);\n                windowState.add(element.getValue());\n\n                triggerContext.key = key;\n                triggerContext.window = window;\n\n                TriggerResult triggerResult = triggerContext.onElement(element);\n\n                if (triggerResult.isFire()) {\n                    ACC contents = windowState.get();\n                    if (contents != null) {\n                        emitWindowContents(window, contents);\n                    }\n                }\n\n                if (triggerResult.isPurge()) {\n                    windowState.clear();\n                }\n                registerCleanupTimer(window);\n            }\n        }\n\n        // side output input event if\n        // element not handled by any window\n        // late arriving tag has been set\n        // windowAssigner is event time and current timestamp + allowed lateness no less than\n        // element timestamp\n        if (isSkippedElement && isElementLate(element)) {\n            if (lateDataOutputTag != null) {\n                sideOutput(element);\n            } else {\n                this.numLateRecordsDropped.inc();\n            }\n        }\n    }\n\n    @Override\n    public void onEventTime(InternalTimer<K, W> timer) throws Exception {\n        triggerContext.key = timer.getKey();\n        triggerContext.window = timer.getNamespace();\n\n        MergingWindowSet<W> mergingWindows;\n\n        if (windowAssigner instanceof MergingWindowAssigner) {\n            mergingWindows = getMergingWindowSet();\n            W stateWindow = mergingWindows.getStateWindow(triggerContext.window);\n            if (stateWindow == null) {\n                // Timer firing for non-existent window, this can only happen if a\n                // trigger did not clean up timers. We have already cleared the merging\n                // window and therefore the Trigger state, however, so nothing to do.\n                return;\n            } else {\n                windowState.setCurrentNamespace(stateWindow);\n            }\n        } else {\n            windowState.setCurrentNamespace(triggerContext.window);\n            mergingWindows = null;\n        }\n\n        TriggerResult triggerResult = triggerContext.onEventTime(timer.getTimestamp());\n\n        if (triggerResult.isFire()) {\n            ACC contents = windowState.get();\n            if (contents != null) {\n                emitWindowContents(triggerContext.window, contents);\n            }\n        }\n\n        if (triggerResult.isPurge()) {\n            windowState.clear();\n        }\n\n        if (windowAssigner.isEventTime()\n                && isCleanupTime(triggerContext.window, timer.getTimestamp())) {\n            clearAllState(triggerContext.window, windowState, mergingWindows);\n        }\n\n        if (mergingWindows != null) {\n            // need to make sure to update the merging state in state\n            mergingWindows.persist();\n        }\n    }\n\n    @Override\n    public void onProcessingTime(InternalTimer<K, W> timer) throws Exception {\n        triggerContext.key = timer.getKey();\n        triggerContext.window = timer.getNamespace();\n\n        MergingWindowSet<W> mergingWindows;\n\n        if (windowAssigner instanceof MergingWindowAssigner) {\n            mergingWindows = getMergingWindowSet();\n            W stateWindow = mergingWindows.getStateWindow(triggerContext.window);\n            if (stateWindow == null) {\n                // Timer firing for non-existent window, this can only happen if a\n                // trigger did not clean up timers. We have already cleared the merging\n                // window and therefore the Trigger state, however, so nothing to do.\n                return;\n            } else {\n                windowState.setCurrentNamespace(stateWindow);\n            }\n        } else {\n            windowState.setCurrentNamespace(triggerContext.window);\n            mergingWindows = null;\n        }\n\n        TriggerResult triggerResult = triggerContext.onProcessingTime(timer.getTimestamp());\n\n        if (triggerResult.isFire()) {\n            ACC contents = windowState.get();\n            if (contents != null) {\n                emitWindowContents(triggerContext.window, contents);\n            }\n        }\n\n        if (triggerResult.isPurge()) {\n            windowState.clear();\n        }\n\n        if (!windowAssigner.isEventTime()\n                && isCleanupTime(triggerContext.window, timer.getTimestamp())) {\n            clearAllState(triggerContext.window, windowState, mergingWindows);\n        }\n\n        if (mergingWindows != null) {\n            // need to make sure to update the merging state in state\n            mergingWindows.persist();\n        }\n    }\n\n    @Override\n    public OperatorAttributes getOperatorAttributes() {\n        boolean isOutputOnlyAfterEndOfStream =\n                windowAssigner instanceof GlobalWindows\n                        && trigger instanceof GlobalWindows.EndOfStreamTrigger;\n        return new OperatorAttributesBuilder()\n                .setOutputOnlyAfterEndOfStream(isOutputOnlyAfterEndOfStream)\n                .build();\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Drops all state for the given window and calls {@link Trigger#clear(Window,\n     * Trigger.TriggerContext)}.\n     *\n     * <p>The caller must ensure that the correct key is set in the state backend and the\n     * triggerContext object.\n     */\n    private void clearAllState(\n            W window, AppendingState<IN, ACC> windowState, MergingWindowSet<W> mergingWindows)\n            throws Exception {\n        windowState.clear();\n        triggerContext.clear();\n        processContext.window = window;\n        processContext.clear();\n        if (mergingWindows != null) {\n            mergingWindows.retireWindow(window);\n            mergingWindows.persist();\n        }\n    }\n\n    /** Emits the contents of the given window using the {@link InternalWindowFunction}. */\n    @SuppressWarnings(\"unchecked\")\n    private void emitWindowContents(W window, ACC contents) throws Exception {\n        timestampedCollector.setAbsoluteTimestamp(window.maxTimestamp());\n        processContext.window = window;\n        userFunction.process(\n                triggerContext.key, window, processContext, contents, timestampedCollector);\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Write skipped late arriving element to SideOutput.\n     *\n     * @param element skipped late arriving element to side output\n     */\n    protected void sideOutput(StreamRecord<IN> element) {\n        output.collect(lateDataOutputTag, element);\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Retrieves the {@link MergingWindowSet} for the currently active key. The caller must ensure\n     * that the correct key is set in the state backend.\n     *\n     * <p>The caller must also ensure to properly persist changes to state using {@link\n     * MergingWindowSet#persist()}.\n     */\n    protected MergingWindowSet<W> getMergingWindowSet() throws Exception {\n        @SuppressWarnings(\"unchecked\")\n        MergingWindowAssigner<? super IN, W> mergingAssigner =\n                (MergingWindowAssigner<? super IN, W>) windowAssigner;\n        return new MergingWindowSet<>(mergingAssigner, mergingSetsState);\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Returns {@code true} if the watermark is after the end timestamp plus the allowed lateness of\n     * the given window.\n     */\n    protected boolean isWindowLate(W window) {\n        return (windowAssigner.isEventTime()\n                && (cleanupTime(window) <= internalTimerService.currentWatermark()));\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Decide if a record is currently late, based on current watermark and allowed lateness.\n     *\n     * @param element The element to check\n     * @return The element for which should be considered when sideoutputs\n     */\n    protected boolean isElementLate(StreamRecord<IN> element) {\n        return (windowAssigner.isEventTime())\n                && (element.getTimestamp() + allowedLateness\n                        <= internalTimerService.currentWatermark());\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Registers a timer to cleanup the content of the window.\n     *\n     * @param window the window whose state to discard\n     */\n    protected void registerCleanupTimer(W window) {\n        long cleanupTime = cleanupTime(window);\n        if (cleanupTime == Long.MAX_VALUE) {\n            // don't set a GC timer for \"end of time\"\n            return;\n        }\n\n        if (windowAssigner.isEventTime()) {\n            triggerContext.registerEventTimeTimer(cleanupTime);\n        } else {\n            triggerContext.registerProcessingTimeTimer(cleanupTime);\n        }\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Deletes the cleanup timer set for the contents of the provided window.\n     *\n     * @param window the window whose state to discard\n     */\n    protected void deleteCleanupTimer(W window) {\n        long cleanupTime = cleanupTime(window);\n        if (cleanupTime == Long.MAX_VALUE) {\n            // no need to clean up because we didn't set one\n            return;\n        }\n        if (windowAssigner.isEventTime()) {\n            triggerContext.deleteEventTimeTimer(cleanupTime);\n        } else {\n            triggerContext.deleteProcessingTimeTimer(cleanupTime);\n        }\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Returns the cleanup time for a window, which is {@code window.maxTimestamp +\n     * allowedLateness}. In case this leads to a value greater than {@link Long#MAX_VALUE} then a\n     * cleanup time of {@link Long#MAX_VALUE} is returned.\n     *\n     * @param window the window whose cleanup time we are computing.\n     */\n    private long cleanupTime(W window) {\n        if (windowAssigner.isEventTime()) {\n            long cleanupTime = window.maxTimestamp() + allowedLateness;\n            return cleanupTime >= window.maxTimestamp() ? cleanupTime : Long.MAX_VALUE;\n        } else {\n            return window.maxTimestamp();\n        }\n    }\n\n    /** Returns {@code true} if the given time is the cleanup time for the given window. */\n    protected final boolean isCleanupTime(W window, long time) {\n        return time == cleanupTime(window);\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Base class for per-window {@link KeyedStateStore KeyedStateStores}. Used to allow per-window\n     * state access for {@link\n     * org.apache.flink.streaming.api.functions.windowing.ProcessWindowFunction}.\n     */\n    public abstract class AbstractPerWindowStateStore extends DefaultKeyedStateStore {\n\n        // we have this in the base class even though it's not used in MergingKeyStore so that\n        // we can always set it and ignore what actual implementation we have\n        protected W window;\n\n        public AbstractPerWindowStateStore(\n                KeyedStateBackend<?> keyedStateBackend, ExecutionConfig executionConfig) {\n            super(\n                    keyedStateBackend,\n                    new SerializerFactory() {\n                        @Override\n                        public <T> TypeSerializer<T> createSerializer(\n                                TypeInformation<T> typeInformation) {\n                            return typeInformation.createSerializer(\n                                    executionConfig.getSerializerConfig());\n                        }\n                    });\n        }\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Special {@link AbstractPerWindowStateStore} that doesn't allow access to per-window state.\n     */\n    public class MergingWindowStateStore extends AbstractPerWindowStateStore {\n\n        public MergingWindowStateStore(\n                KeyedStateBackend<?> keyedStateBackend, ExecutionConfig executionConfig) {\n            super(keyedStateBackend, executionConfig);\n        }\n\n        @Override\n        public <T> ValueState<T> getState(ValueStateDescriptor<T> stateProperties) {\n            throw new UnsupportedOperationException(\n                    \"Per-window state is not allowed when using merging windows.\");\n        }\n\n        @Override\n        public <T> ListState<T> getListState(ListStateDescriptor<T> stateProperties) {\n            throw new UnsupportedOperationException(\n                    \"Per-window state is not allowed when using merging windows.\");\n        }\n\n        @Override\n        public <T> ReducingState<T> getReducingState(ReducingStateDescriptor<T> stateProperties) {\n            throw new UnsupportedOperationException(\n                    \"Per-window state is not allowed when using merging windows.\");\n        }\n\n        @Override\n        public <IN, ACC, OUT> AggregatingState<IN, OUT> getAggregatingState(\n                AggregatingStateDescriptor<IN, ACC, OUT> stateProperties) {\n            throw new UnsupportedOperationException(\n                    \"Per-window state is not allowed when using merging windows.\");\n        }\n\n        @Override\n        public <UK, UV> MapState<UK, UV> getMapState(MapStateDescriptor<UK, UV> stateProperties) {\n            throw new UnsupportedOperationException(\n                    \"Per-window state is not allowed when using merging windows.\");\n        }\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Regular per-window state store for use with {@link\n     * org.apache.flink.streaming.api.functions.windowing.ProcessWindowFunction}.\n     */\n    public class PerWindowStateStore extends AbstractPerWindowStateStore {\n\n        public PerWindowStateStore(\n                KeyedStateBackend<?> keyedStateBackend, ExecutionConfig executionConfig) {\n            super(keyedStateBackend, executionConfig);\n        }\n\n        @Override\n        protected <S extends State> S getPartitionedState(StateDescriptor<S, ?> stateDescriptor)\n                throws Exception {\n            return keyedStateBackend.getPartitionedState(window, windowSerializer, stateDescriptor);\n        }\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * A utility class for handling {@code ProcessWindowFunction} invocations. We keep a mapping from in-flight window to\n * state window that can be queried using {@link #getStateWindow(Window)}.\n *\n * <p>A new window can be added to the set of in-flight windows using {@link #addWindow(Window,\n * MergeFunction)}. This might merge other windows and the caller must react accordingly in the\n * {@link MergeFunction#merge(Object, Collection, Object, Collection)} and adjust the outside view\n * of windows and state.\n *\n * <p>Windows can be removed from the set of windows using {@link #retireWindow(Window)}.\n *\n * @param <W> The type of {@code Window} that this set is keeping track of.\n */\npublic class MergingWindowSet<W extends Window> {\n\n    private static final Logger LOG = LoggerFactory.getLogger(MergingWindowSet.class);\n\n    /**\n     * Mapping from window to the window that keeps the window state. In that case, the provided {@link MergeFunction} is\n     * called.\n     *\n     * <p>This returns the window that is the representative of the added window after adding. This\n     * can either be the new window itself, if no merge occurred, or the newly merged window. Adding\n     * an element to a window or calling trigger functions should only happen on the returned\n     * representative. mergedWindows.size() == 1)) {\n                mergeFunction.merge(\n                        mergeResult,\n                        mergedWindows,\n                        this.mapping.get(mergeResult),\n                        mergedStateWindows);\n            }\n        }\n\n        // the new window created a new, self-contained window without merging\n        if Dropping the element if the window is late (line 408-409)\n     - Setting `isSkippedElement = false` only after successfully processing (line 411)\n     - This allows the final check at line 440 to properly side-output\n\n**The Core Problem**:\n\nIn merging windows, when a **merge causes a window to become late**:\n- The element is never added to the window state (because we continue at line 371)\n- But `isSkippedElement` remains `true` \n- The element is only side-output if it ALSO meets `isElementLate()` criteria based on its own timestamp\n- However, the element might not be \"late\" by its timestamp but the merged window it was assigned to is late\n- This means **late elements can be silently dropped without being side-output** in session/merging window scenarios\n\n### Evidence in Code\n\n**WindowOperator.java lines 303-373**:\n```java\nif (windowAssigner instanceof MergingWindowAssigner) {\n    MergingWindowSet<W> mergingWindows = getMergingWindowSet();\n    \n    for (W window : elementWindows) {\n        // ... merge happens ...\n        \n        // drop if the window is already late\n        if (isWindowLate(actualWindow)) {\n            mergingWindows.retireWindow(actualWindow);\n            continue;  // <-- ELEMENT DROPPED WITHOUT BEING MARKED AS SKIPPED!\n        }\n        isSkippedElement = false;  // <-- ONLY SET IF WINDOW IS NOT LATE\n```\n\n**EvictingWindowOperator.java shows identical pattern** (lines 123-192)\n\n### Missing Comment/TODO\n\nThe code lacks any TODO or FIXME comment indicating awareness of this issue, but there IS evidence that the developers understood merging window late element handling can be problematic:\n\n**WindowOperatorContractTest.java line 1877-1878**:\n```java\n/**\n * A misbehaving {@code WindowAssigner} can cause a window to become late by merging if it moves\n * the end-of-window time before the watermark. WindowAssigner} that assigns elements to sessions\n     * based on the element timestamp.\n     *\n     * @param sessionWindowTimeGapExtractor The extractor to use to extract the time gap from the\n     *     input elements\n     * @return The policy.\n     */\n    @PublicEvolving\n    public static <T> DynamicEventTimeSessionWindows<T> withDynamicGap(\n            SessionWindowTimeGapExtractor<T> logic for windowing based on a {@link WindowAssigner} and {@link\n * Trigger}.\n *\n * <p>When an element arrives it gets assigned a key using a {@link KeySelector} and it gets\n * assigned to zero or more windows using a {@link WindowAssigner}. Based on this, the element is\n * put into panes. A pane is the bucket of elements that have the same key and same {@code Window}.\n * An element can be in multiple panes if it was assigned to multiple windows by the {@code\n * WindowAssigner}.\n *\n * <p>Each pane gets its own instance of the provided {@code Trigger}. This trigger determines when\n * the contents of the pane should be processed to emit results. When a trigger fires, the given\n * {@link InternalWindowFunction} is invoked to produce the results that are emitted for the pane to\n * which the {@code Trigger} belongs.\n *\n * @param <K> The type of key returned by the {@code KeySelector}.\n * @param <IN> The type of the incoming elements.\n * @param <OUT> The type of elements emitted by the {@code InternalWindowFunction}.\n * @param <W> The type of {@code Window} that the {@code WindowAssigner} assigns.\n */\n@Internal\npublic class WindowOperator<K, IN, ACC, OUT, W extends Window>\n        extends AbstractUdfStreamOperator<OUT, InternalWindowFunction<ACC, OUT, K, W>>\n        implements OneInputStreamOperator<IN, OUT>, Triggerable<K, W> {\n\n    private static final long serialVersionUID = 1L;\n\n    // ------------------------------------------------------------------------\n    // Configuration values and user functions\n    // ------------------------------------------------------------------------\n\n    protected final WindowAssigner<? super IN, W> windowAssigner;\n\n    private final KeySelector<IN, K> keySelector;\n\n    private final Trigger<? super IN, ? super W> trigger;\n\n    private final StateDescriptor<? extends AppendingState<IN, ACC>, ?> windowStateDescriptor;\n\n    /** For serializing the key in checkpoints. */\n    protected final TypeSerializer<K> keySerializer;\n\n    /** For serializing the window in checkpoints. */\n    protected final TypeSerializer<W> windowSerializer;\n\n    /**\n     * The allowed lateness for elements. This is used for:\n     *\n     * <ul>\n     *   <li>Deciding if an element should be dropped from a window due to lateness.\n     *   <li>Clearing the state of a window if the system time passes the {@code window.maxTimestamp\n     *       + allowedLateness} landmark.\n     * </ul>\n     */\n    protected final long allowedLateness;\n\n    /**\n     * {@link OutputTag} to use for late arriving events. Elements for which {@code\n     * window.maxTimestamp + allowedLateness} is smaller than the current watermark will be emitted\n     * to this.\n     */\n    protected final OutputTag<IN> lateDataOutputTag;\n\n    private static final String LATE_ELEMENTS_DROPPED_METRIC_NAME = \"numLateRecordsDropped\";\n\n    protected transient Counter numLateRecordsDropped;\n\n    // ------------------------------------------------------------------------\n    // State that is not checkpointed\n    // ------------------------------------------------------------------------\n\n    /** The state in which the window contents is stored. Each window is a namespace */\n    private transient InternalAppendingState<K, W, IN, ACC, ACC> windowState;\n\n    /**\n     * The {@link #windowState}, typed to merging state for merging windows. Null if the window\n     * state is not mergeable.\n     */\n    private transient InternalMergingState<K, W, IN, ACC, ACC> windowMergingState;\n\n    /** The state that holds the merging window metadata (the sets that describe what is merged). */\n    private transient InternalListState<K, VoidNamespace, Tuple2<W, W>> mergingSetsState;\n\n    /**\n     * This is given to the {@code InternalWindowFunction} for emitting elements with a given\n     * timestamp.\n     */\n    protected transient TimestampedCollector<OUT> timestampedCollector;\n\n    protected transient Context triggerContext = new Context(null, null);\n\n    protected transient WindowContext processContext;\n\n    protected transient WindowAssigner.WindowAssignerContext windowAssignerContext;\n\n    // ------------------------------------------------------------------------\n    // State that needs to be checkpointed\n    // ------------------------------------------------------------------------\n\n    protected transient InternalTimerService<W> internalTimerService;\n\n    /** Creates a new {@code WindowOperator} based on the given policies and user functions. */\n    public WindowOperator(\n            WindowAssigner<? super IN, W> windowAssigner,\n            TypeSerializer<W> windowSerializer,\n            KeySelector<IN, K> keySelector,\n            TypeSerializer<K> keySerializer,\n            StateDescriptor<? extends AppendingState<IN, ACC>, ?> windowStateDescriptor,\n            InternalWindowFunction<ACC, OUT, K, W> windowFunction,\n            Trigger<? super IN, ? super W> trigger,\n            long allowedLateness,\n            OutputTag<IN> lateDataOutputTag) {\n\n        super(windowFunction);\n\n        checkArgument(allowedLateness >= 0);\n\n        checkArgument(\n                windowStateDescriptor == null || windowStateDescriptor.isSerializerInitialized(),\n                \"window state serializer is not properly initialized\");\n\n        this.windowAssigner = checkNotNull(windowAssigner);\n        this.windowSerializer = checkNotNull(windowSerializer);\n        this.keySelector = checkNotNull(keySelector);\n        this.keySerializer = checkNotNull(keySerializer);\n        this.windowStateDescriptor = windowStateDescriptor;\n        this.trigger = checkNotNull(trigger);\n        this.allowedLateness = allowedLateness;\n        this.lateDataOutputTag = lateDataOutputTag;\n    }\n\n    @Override\n    public void setup(\n            StreamTask<?, ?> containingTask,\n            StreamConfig config,\n            Output<StreamRecord<OUT>> output) {\n        super.setup(containingTask, config, output);\n    }\n\n    @Override\n    public void setProcessingTimeService(ProcessingTimeService processingTimeService) {\n        super.setProcessingTimeService(processingTimeService);\n    }\n\n    @Override\n    public void open() throws Exception {\n        super.open();\n\n        this.numLateRecordsDropped = metrics.counter(LATE_ELEMENTS_DROPPED_METRIC_NAME);\n        timestampedCollector = new TimestampedCollector<>(output);\n\n        internalTimerService = getInternalTimerService(\"window-timers\", windowSerializer, this);\n\n        triggerContext = new Context(null, null);\n        processContext = new WindowContext(null);\n\n        windowAssignerContext =\n                new WindowAssigner.WindowAssignerContext() {\n                    @Override\n                    public long getCurrentProcessingTime() {\n                        return internalTimerService.currentProcessingTime();\n                    }\n                };\n\n        // create (or restore) the state that hold the actual window contents\n        // NOTE - the state may be null in the case of the overriding evicting window operator\n        if (windowStateDescriptor != null) {\n            windowState =\n                    (InternalAppendingState<K, W, IN, ACC, ACC>)\n                            getOrCreateKeyedState(windowSerializer, windowStateDescriptor);\n        }\n\n        // create the typed and helper states for merging windows\n        if (windowAssigner instanceof MergingWindowAssigner) {\n\n            // store a typed reference for the state of merging windows - sanity check\n            if (windowState instanceof InternalMergingState) {\n                windowMergingState = (InternalMergingState<K, W, IN, ACC, ACC>) windowState;\n            } else if (windowState != null) {\n     @Test
    void testLateElementMergingSessionWindowsSideOutput() throws Exception {
        // Test for late element side output with merging/session windows
        // Bug: When an element arrives late and could extend a session window,
        // it should be side-output as a late element if all windows it's assigned to are late
        final int gapSize = 3;
        final long lateness = 0;
